SELECT
    if(sellCurrencyId<buyCurrencyId,concat(sellSymbol,':',buySymbol),concat(buySymbol,':',sellSymbol)) pairs,
    count() trades
FROM analytics.trades
WHERE contract_type='DEX/Kyber Network v2'
GROUP BY pairs
HAVING trades>100
ORDER BY trades DESC


SELECT * FROM
(

SELECT
    toStartOfHour(tx_time) time,
    toUInt32(time) time_i,
    sum(amountBuy)/sum(amountSell) rate,
    sum(amountSell) from_amount,
    sum(amountBuy) to_amount,
    min(amountBuy/amountSell) low,
    max(amountBuy/amountSell) high,
    argMin(amountBuy/amountSell, tx_time) open,
    argMax(amountBuy/amountSell, tx_time) close
FROM analytics.trades
WHERE contract_type='DEX/Kyber Network v2'
AND sellSymbol='ETH' AND buySymbol='BAT'
GROUP BY time

UNION ALL

SELECT
    toStartOfHour(tx_time) time,
    toUInt32(time) time_i,
    sum(amountSell)/sum(amountBuy) rate,
    sum(amountBuy) from_amount,
    sum(amountSell) to_amount,
    min(amountSell/amountBuy) low,
    max(amountSell/amountBuy) high,
    argMin(amountSell/amountBuy, tx_time) open,
    argMax(amountSell/amountBuy, tx_time) close

FROM analytics.trades
WHERE contract_type='DEX/Kyber Network v2'
AND sellSymbol='BAT' AND buySymbol='ETH'
GROUP BY time

)

ORDER BY time
